<p><b>N'Golo Kanté</b> (born 29 March 1991) is a French professional <a href="/wiki/Association_football" title="Association football">footballer</a> who plays as a <a href="/wiki/Central_midfielder" class="mw-redirect" title="Central midfielder">central midfielder</a> for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> and the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France national team</a>.
</p><p>Upon making his senior professional debut with <a href="/wiki/US_Boulogne" title="US Boulogne">Boulogne</a> in 2012, appearing as a substitute in one <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Ligue_2" title="2011–12 Ligue 2">Ligue 2</a> match and played an entire season in the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Championnat_National" title="2012–13 Championnat National">third division</a> the following year. After that he joined <a href="/wiki/2013%E2%80%9314_Ligue_2" title="2013–14 Ligue 2">League 2</a> side <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> on a free transfer, finished third and won promotion to the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a>.  He stayed with the club for one more year.
</p><p>In 2015, he joined <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> for a fee worth £5.6&#160;million and became an integral member of the club's first <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Premier_League#League_table" title="2015–16 Premier League">Premier League title</a>. He was named <a href="/wiki/List_of_Leicester_City_F.C._players#Players.27_Player_of_the_Year" title="List of Leicester City F.C. players">Leicester City's Player of the Year</a> in his first, and only, <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Leicester_City_F.C._season" title="2015–16 Leicester City F.C. season">season at the club</a>. The following year, he joined Chelsea for a fee worth £32&#160;million and won the league; making him the first outfield player to win back-to-back English league titles with different clubs since <a href="/wiki/Eric_Cantona" title="Eric Cantona">Eric Cantona</a> in <a href="/wiki/1991%E2%80%9392_Football_League_First_Division#League_standings" title="1991–92 Football League First Division">1992</a> and <a href="/wiki/1992%E2%80%9393_FA_Premier_League#League_table" title="1992–93 FA Premier League">1993</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-4">&#91;4&#93;</a></sup> He has also won the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a> and <a href="/wiki/FWA_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="FWA Footballer of the Year">FWA Footballer of the Year</a> award.
</p><p>Kanté made his senior international debut for France in 2016 and was included in the squad that finished runners-up at the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016" title="UEFA Euro 2016">2016 European Championship</a>. In 2017 Kanté was named the <a href="/wiki/French_Player_of_the_Year" title="French Player of the Year">French Player of the Year</a>, a first for a player from the Premier League in seven years, and 12 months later was a key member of the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> winning <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_squads#France" title="2018 FIFA World Cup squads">squad</a>.
</p>

<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-16"><a href="#Honours"><span class="tocnumber">6</span> <span class="toctext">Honours</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-17"><a href="#References"><span class="tocnumber">7</span> <span class="toctext">References</span></a></li>
<li class="toclevel-1 tocsection-18"><a href="#External_links"><span class="tocnumber">8</span> <span class="toctext">External links</span></a></li>
</ul>
</div>

<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Club_career">Club career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: Club career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Boulogne">Boulogne</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Boulogne">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Born in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> to <a href="/wiki/Mali" title="Mali">Malian</a> parents,<sup id="cite_ref-:3_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> Kanté began his career at the age of eight at JS Suresnes in the western suburbs of the capital, remaining there for a decade. According to assistant manager Pierre Ville, Kanté remained outside the radar of big teams because of his small stature and selfless style of play.<sup id="cite_ref-how_6-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-how-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> Through the contacts of Suresnes' president in 2010, he joined the reserve team of <a href="/wiki/US_Boulogne" title="US Boulogne">Boulogne</a>. He made his professional debut in the last game of the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_2" title="Ligue 2">Ligue 2</a> <a href="/wiki/2011%E2%80%9312_Ligue_2" title="2011–12 Ligue 2">season</a> on 18 May 2012, a 1–2 home defeat for his already relegated team to <a href="/wiki/AS_Monaco_FC" title="AS Monaco FC">Monaco</a>, replacing <a href="/wiki/Virgile_Reset" title="Virgile Reset">Virgile Reset</a> for the final 11 minutes.<sup id="cite_ref-soccerway2_7-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-soccerway2-7">&#91;7&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>During the <a href="/wiki/2012%E2%80%9313_Championnat_National" title="2012–13 Championnat National">2012–13 season</a>, he played in the third-tier <a href="/wiki/Championnat_National" title="Championnat National">Championnat National</a>, missing only one league game. On 10 August, he scored his first senior goal, the only one in a win over <a href="/wiki/US_Luzenac" class="mw-redirect" title="US Luzenac">Luzenac</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_la_Lib%C3%A9ration" title="Stade de la Libération">Stade de la Libération</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-voix_8-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-voix-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup> and he added two more over the campaign.
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Caen">Caen</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Caen">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Kant%C3%A9.png" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Kant%C3%A9.png/170px-Kant%C3%A9.png" decoding="async" width="170" height="255" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Kant%C3%A9.png/255px-Kant%C3%A9.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/5a/Kant%C3%A9.png/340px-Kant%C3%A9.png 2x" data-file-width="1512" data-file-height="2268" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Kant%C3%A9.png" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kanté with <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> in 2013</div></div></div>
<p>In 2013, he joined Ligue 2 side <a href="/wiki/Stade_Malherbe_Caen" title="Stade Malherbe Caen">Caen</a> and played all 38 games in his first season as they came third in Ligue 2, earning them promotion to <a href="/wiki/Ligue_1" title="Ligue 1">Ligue 1</a>. In his second match on 9 August, he scored his first goal to equalise in a 2–1 win at <a href="/wiki/Stade_Lavallois" title="Stade Lavallois">Laval</a>;<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9">&#91;9&#93;</a></sup> he levelled again with his other goal of the campaign on 11 April 2014, in a 3–2 win at <a href="/wiki/FC_Istres" title="FC Istres">Istres</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10">&#91;10&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p><a href="/wiki/2014%E2%80%9315_Ligue_1" title="2014–15 Ligue 1">The following season</a>, Kanté played 37 games as Caen remained in the top flight; his one absence was suspension through being sent off in a 0–1 home loss to <a href="/wiki/Stade_Rennais_F.C." title="Stade Rennais F.C.">Rennes</a> on 30 August.<sup id="cite_ref-11" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-11">&#91;11&#93;</a></sup> Three weeks earlier, he scored their first goal of the season in a 3–0 win at <a href="/wiki/Evian_Thonon_Gaillard_F.C." class="mw-redirect" title="Evian Thonon Gaillard F.C.">Evian</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-12" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-12">&#91;12&#93;</a></sup> He recovered the ball more times over the season than any other player in Europe.<sup id="cite_ref-how_6-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-how-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Leicester_City">Leicester City</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Leicester City">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>Kanté was scouted for <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a> club <a href="/wiki/Leicester_City_F.C." title="Leicester City F.C.">Leicester City</a> by <a href="/wiki/Steve_Walsh_(scout)" title="Steve Walsh (scout)">Steve Walsh</a>, who had previously facilitated the transfers of <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Vardy" title="Jamie Vardy">Jamie Vardy</a> and <a href="/wiki/Riyad_Mahrez" title="Riyad Mahrez">Riyad Mahrez</a> to the team.<sup id="cite_ref-13" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-13">&#91;13&#93;</a></sup> On 3 August 2015, he joined Leicester on a four-year contract, for an undisclosed fee reported to be worth €8&#160;million (£5.6&#160;million).<sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14">&#91;14&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-15" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-15">&#91;15&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut five days later by replacing Vardy for the final eight minutes of a 4–2 home win over <a href="/wiki/Sunderland_A.F.C." title="Sunderland A.F.C.">Sunderland</a>. On 7 November, he scored his first Premier League goal in a 2–1 home win against <a href="/wiki/Watford_F.C." title="Watford F.C.">Watford</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16">&#91;16&#93;</a></sup> He was identified as the successor to <a href="/wiki/Esteban_Cambiasso" title="Esteban Cambiasso">Esteban Cambiasso</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_17-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He earned much praise and many plaudits for his consistently impressive displays for Leicester, and was widely considered to be a major factor in the club's excellent form as they went on to win the <a href="/wiki/2015%E2%80%9316_Premier_League" title="2015–16 Premier League">2015–16 Premier League</a>, consistently making a high number of tackles and interceptions.<sup id="cite_ref-18" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-18">&#91;18&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19">&#91;19&#93;</a></sup> In April, he was one of four Leicester players named in the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Team_of_the_Year_(2010s)#2015–16" title="PFA Team of the Year (2010s)">PFA Team of the Year</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PFA1516_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFA1516-20">&#91;20&#93;</a></sup> By the end of the season, Kanté had managed 175 tackles (31 more than any other player) and 157 interceptions (15 more than any other player), topping the defensive stats at the end of the 2015–16 Premier League season.<sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21">&#91;21&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kanté was the only key member of the squad to leave the club in the summer of 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-Claudio_Ranieri_urges_Leicester_fans_to_welcome_N&#39;Golo_Kante_on_return_22-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Claudio_Ranieri_urges_Leicester_fans_to_welcome_N&#39;Golo_Kante_on_return-22">&#91;22&#93;</a></sup> His departure proved a major factor in Leicester's sharp decline in form in the 2016–17 season, as the club was unable to find an equally skilled midfielder to replace him.<sup id="cite_ref-23" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-23">&#91;23&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Chelsea">Chelsea</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Chelsea">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<h4><span id="2016.E2.80.9317:_Back-to-back_league_champion"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2016–17:_Back-to-back_league_champion">2016–17: Back-to-back league champion</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: 2016–17: Back-to-back league champion">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:172px;"><a href="/wiki/File:Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg/170px-Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg" decoding="async" width="170" height="313" class="thumbimage" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg/255px-Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/32/Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg/340px-Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1776" data-file-height="3266" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:Ngolo_Kante_2017.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kanté playing for <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> in 2017</div></div></div>
<p>On 16 July 2016, Kanté signed for <a href="/wiki/Chelsea_F.C." title="Chelsea F.C.">Chelsea</a> for a reported fee of £32&#160;million. After signing a five-year contract with the club, Kanté said: "I am so happy to have signed for one of the biggest clubs in Europe. It’s a dream come true for me."<sup id="cite_ref-24" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-24">&#91;24&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-25" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-25">&#91;25&#93;</a></sup> According to <a href="/wiki/Football_Leaks" title="Football Leaks">Football Leaks</a>, Kanté was offered a deal where a part of his salary would be transferred into an offshore account to avoid taxes. Kanté chose to refuse the deal, with his lawyer stating in an email: "N'golo is flexible, he simply wants a normal salary."<sup id="cite_ref-26" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-26">&#91;26&#93;</a></sup> Kanté was given the number 7 shirt, left vacant since the exit of <a href="/wiki/Ramires" title="Ramires">Ramires</a> in January.<sup id="cite_ref-27" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-27">&#91;27&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 15 August 2016, Kanté made his competitive debut in their season opener against <a href="/wiki/West_Ham_United_F.C." title="West Ham United F.C.">West Ham United</a>. Despite picking up a yellow card in the first three minutes of the game, he shone as the game went on, to help Chelsea to a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28">&#91;28&#93;</a></sup> Three months after his move to London, he faced his former side, Leicester City for the first time, and was Man of the Match in a 3–0 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-29" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-29">&#91;29&#93;</a></sup> On 23 October, he scored his first goal for Chelsea in a 4–0 home win against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_United_F.C." title="Manchester United F.C.">Manchester United</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30">&#91;30&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 26 December 2016, Kanté was named by <i><a href="/wiki/L%27%C3%89quipe" title="L&#39;Équipe">L'Équipe</a></i> as the world's sixth best footballer of 2016.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31">&#91;31&#93;</a></sup> On 13 March 2017, Kanté was named man of the match and scored the only goal in the 51st minute, in an <a href="/wiki/2016%E2%80%9317_FA_Cup" title="2016–17 FA Cup">FA Cup</a> quarter-final win over Manchester United at <a href="/wiki/Stamford_Bridge_(stadium)" title="Stamford Bridge (stadium)">Stamford Bridge</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32">&#91;32&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33">&#91;33&#93;</a></sup> On 20 April, Kanté was named in the PFA Team of the Year for the second consecutive season.<sup id="cite_ref-PFA1617_34-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFA1617-34">&#91;34&#93;</a></sup> He was also later named the <a href="/wiki/PFA_Players%27_Player_of_the_Year" title="PFA Players&#39; Player of the Year">PFA Players' Player of the Year</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-PFAPlayer_35-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PFAPlayer-35">&#91;35&#93;</a></sup> the <a href="/wiki/FWA_Footballer_of_the_Year" title="FWA Footballer of the Year">FWA Footballer of the Year</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-FWAPlayer_36-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-FWAPlayer-36">&#91;36&#93;</a></sup> and the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Player_of_the_Season" title="Premier League Player of the Season">Premier League Player of the Season</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-PremierLeaguePlayer_37-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PremierLeaguePlayer-37">&#91;37&#93;</a></sup> Kanté become the first player since <a href="/wiki/Eric_Cantona" title="Eric Cantona">Eric Cantona</a> in 1993 to win backto-back top-flight titles in England with two clubs.<sup id="cite_ref-38" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-38">&#91;38&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2017.E2.80.9319:_FA_Cup.2C_UEFA_Europa_League_wins"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2017–19:_FA_Cup,_UEFA_Europa_League_wins">2017–19: FA Cup, UEFA Europa League wins</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: 2017–19: FA Cup, UEFA Europa League wins">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>In October 2017, Kanté was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Ballon_d%27Or" title="Ballon d&#39;Or">Ballon d'Or</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-39" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-39">&#91;39&#93;</a></sup> He would go on to gain an <a href="/wiki/FA_Cup" title="FA Cup">FA Cup</a> winners medal, appearing for the whole 90 minutes in a 1–0 victory over Manchester United in the final on 19 May 2018. BBC Sport awarded him the man of the match award.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40">&#91;40&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 23 November 2018, Kanté signed a new five-year contract at Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41">&#91;41&#93;</a></sup> On 24 January, he scored the first goal of Chelsea's 2–1 <a href="/wiki/EFL_Cup" title="EFL Cup">EFL Cup</a> semi-final second leg win at home to <a href="/wiki/Tottenham_Hotspur" class="mw-redirect" title="Tottenham Hotspur">Tottenham Hotspur</a>. The score was tied 2–2 on aggregate at the end of 90 minutes, with Chelsea winning the shootout 4–2.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42">&#91;42&#93;</a></sup> Kanté scored on his 300th club appearance, a 2–2 home draw against Burnley on 22 April.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43">&#91;43&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2019.E2.80.9320:_Injury-hit_season"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2019–20:_Injury-hit_season">2019–20: Injury-hit season</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: 2019–20: Injury-hit season">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>On 11 August 2019, Kanté started the Premier League campaign from the bench as Chelsea suffered a 4–0 away defeat to Manchester United.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44">&#91;44&#93;</a></sup> He has been out for almost a month including missing the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Champions_League" title="UEFA Champions League">Champions League</a> opener against <a href="/wiki/Valencia_CF" title="Valencia CF">Valencia</a> because of ankle injury.<sup id="cite_ref-45" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-45">&#91;45&#93;</a></sup> On 22 September, Kanté scored the only goal in a 1–2 loss against <a href="/wiki/Liverpool_F.C." title="Liverpool F.C.">Liverpool</a> at Stamford Bridge.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46">&#91;46&#93;</a></sup> His first goal of the season was nominated for the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League_Goal_of_the_Month" title="Premier League Goal of the Month">Premier League Goal of the Month</a> award along with his Chelsea teammate, <a href="/wiki/Fikayo_Tomori" title="Fikayo Tomori">Fikayo Tomori</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47">&#91;47&#93;</a></sup> Kanté marked his 150th Chelsea appearance with a goal against <a href="/wiki/Manchester_City_F.C." title="Manchester City F.C.">Manchester City</a>, in a 1–2 away defeat on 23 November.<sup id="cite_ref-48" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-48">&#91;48&#93;</a></sup> Later that month Kanté revealed he decided against moving to <a href="/wiki/Paris_Saint-Germain_F.C." title="Paris Saint-Germain F.C.">PSG</a> and said, "‘Sometimes we do not necessarily know where we want to go, but we know what we have." He said he felt good in London and had faith in the project at Chelsea.<sup id="cite_ref-49" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-49">&#91;49&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>In May 2020 during the <a href="/wiki/COVID-19_pandemic_in_the_United_Kingdom" title="COVID-19 pandemic in the United Kingdom">COVID-19 pandemic</a>, Kanté chose to train from home after Chelsea resumed training on site. The club supported his stance, even if he would miss the rest of the season.<sup id="cite_ref-50" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-50">&#91;50&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h4><span id="2020.E2.80.9321"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="2020–21">2020–21</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: 2020–21">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>Kanté showed an impressive display  in the Premier League opener against <a href="/wiki/Brighton_%26_Hove_Albion_F.C." title="Brighton &amp; Hove Albion F.C.">Brighton &amp; Hove Albion</a>, in a 3–1 away win on 14 September 2020.<sup id="cite_ref-51" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-51">&#91;51&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-52" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-52">&#91;52&#93;</a></sup> On 23 February 2021, Kanté marked his 200th appearance in all competitions with the club as Chelsea beat <a href="/wiki/Atl%C3%A9tico_Madrid" title="Atlético Madrid">Atlético Madrid</a> 1–0 in the Champions League round of 16.<sup id="cite_ref-53" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-53">&#91;53&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-54" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-54">&#91;54&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="International_career">International career</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: International career">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:164px;"><a href="/wiki/File:N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9_Russia_2018.jpg" class="image"><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/2/2e/N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9_Russia_2018.jpg" decoding="async" width="162" height="411" class="thumbimage" data-file-width="162" data-file-height="411" /></a>  <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a href="/wiki/File:N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9_Russia_2018.jpg" class="internal" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Kanté lining up for <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France</a> at the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a></div></div></div>
<p>Born to Malian parents, Kanté was approached by <a href="/wiki/Mali_national_football_team" title="Mali national football team">Mali</a> ahead of the <a href="/wiki/2015_Africa_Cup_of_Nations" title="2015 Africa Cup of Nations">2015 Africa Cup of Nations</a> having not played for France in any of their age group teams. Kanté declined on the basis that he was still trying to establish himself in Ligue 1.<sup id="cite_ref-55" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-55">&#91;55&#93;</a></sup> Mali issued a further invitation to Kanté in January 2016,<sup id="cite_ref-56" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-56">&#91;56&#93;</a></sup> although he stated that he was still undecided about which national team to represent should he get an invite from France.<sup id="cite_ref-57" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-57">&#91;57&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 March 2016, Kanté was selected for the <a href="/wiki/France_national_football_team" title="France national football team">France senior squad</a> for the first time to face the <a href="/wiki/Netherlands_national_football_team" title="Netherlands national football team">Netherlands</a> and <a href="/wiki/Russia_national_football_team" title="Russia national football team">Russia</a> in friendlies.<sup id="cite_ref-58" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-58">&#91;58&#93;</a></sup> He made his debut against the former eight days later, replacing <a href="/wiki/Lassana_Diarra" title="Lassana Diarra">Lassana Diarra</a> at half time in a 3–2 win at the <a href="/wiki/Amsterdam_Arena" class="mw-redirect" title="Amsterdam Arena">Amsterdam Arena</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-59" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-59">&#91;59&#93;</a></sup> On his 25th birthday, 29 March, he made his first start and scored to open a 4–2 win over Russia at the <a href="/wiki/Stade_de_France" title="Stade de France">Stade de France</a>; fellow birthday celebrant <a href="/wiki/Dimitri_Payet" title="Dimitri Payet">Dimitri Payet</a> also scored.<sup id="cite_ref-60" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-60">&#91;60&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 10 June 2016, Kanté appeared in his first competitive match for France by starting the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_Group_A" title="UEFA Euro 2016 Group A">opening match of Euro 2016</a> against <a href="/wiki/Romania_national_football_team" title="Romania national football team">Romania</a>; he played the entire match, made the most passes, the most tackles, the most interceptions, covered the most distance on the pitch and <a href="/wiki/Assist_(football)" class="mw-redirect" title="Assist (football)">assisted</a> Dimitri Payet's winning goal in a 2–1 victory.<sup id="cite_ref-61" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-61">&#91;61&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-62" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-62">&#91;62&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-63" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-63">&#91;63&#93;</a></sup> In the <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_knockout_phase" title="UEFA Euro 2016 knockout phase">round of 16 match</a> against the <a href="/wiki/Republic_of_Ireland_national_football_team" title="Republic of Ireland national football team">Republic of Ireland</a> at the <a href="/wiki/Parc_Olympique_Lyonnais" title="Parc Olympique Lyonnais">Parc Olympique Lyonnais</a>, Kanté picked up a yellow card in the 27th minute (his second of Euro 2016 which would cause him to be suspended from the quarter-final) and was replaced with <a href="/wiki/Kingsley_Coman" title="Kingsley Coman">Kingsley Coman</a> in the 46th minute with the French trailing 0–1 at half time.<sup id="cite_ref-64" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-64">&#91;64&#93;</a></sup> Kanté was unused in <a href="/wiki/UEFA_Euro_2016_Final" title="UEFA Euro 2016 Final">the final</a>, which France lost 1–0 to <a href="/wiki/Portugal_national_football_team" title="Portugal national football team">Portugal</a> after extra time.<sup id="cite_ref-65" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-65">&#91;65&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>On 17 May 2018, he was called up to the 23-man <a href="/wiki/French_national_football_team" class="mw-redirect" title="French national football team">French squad</a> for the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup" title="2018 FIFA World Cup">2018 FIFA World Cup</a> in Russia.<sup id="cite_ref-66" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-66">&#91;66&#93;</a></sup> He featured in all 7 matches for France in the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-67" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-67">&#91;67&#93;</a></sup> He was awarded <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_statistics#Man_of_the_Match" title="2018 FIFA World Cup statistics">man-of-the-match</a>  against Denmark in the group stage and on 15 July, Kanté started in France's 4–2 win over <a href="/wiki/Croatia_national_football_team" title="Croatia national football team">Croatia</a> in the <a href="/wiki/2018_FIFA_World_Cup_Final" title="2018 FIFA World Cup Final">final</a> of the tournament.<sup id="cite_ref-McNulty1_68-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-McNulty1-68">&#91;68&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Style_of_play">Style of play</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Style of play">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>A dynamic, diminutive and disciplined player,<sup id="cite_ref-69" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-69">&#91;69&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-best_midfielder_70-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_midfielder-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-71" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-71">&#91;71&#93;</a></sup> Kanté is known for his relentless energy and excellent ball-winning abilities as a <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Box-to-box_midfielder" title="Midfielder">box-to-box midfielder</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-10_best_central_midfielders_72-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-10_best_central_midfielders-72">&#91;72&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Disappointing_lack_of_deep-lying_playmakers_in_the_Premier_League_73-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Disappointing_lack_of_deep-lying_playmakers_in_the_Premier_League-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Man_of_the_year_N’Golo_Kante_74-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Man_of_the_year_N’Golo_Kante-74">&#91;74&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-complete_midfielder_75-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-complete_midfielder-75">&#91;75&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-76" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-76">&#91;76&#93;</a></sup> This is attributed to his strong positional sense, off the ball movement, and ability to read the game.<sup id="cite_ref-next_star_77-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-next_star-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup> His game is considered as, or tasked with, doing the "dirty work," which includes running, fetching, and retrieving possession; to benefit team-mates so they can be put in goal scoring positions. He was a late bloomer and by the age of 21 had only made one senior appearance in the <a href="/wiki/Ligue_2" title="Ligue 2">second tier of French football</a>. He credits his calm and composed demeanor on the pitch to his gradual rise through <a href="/wiki/French_football_league_system" title="French football league system">three levels in the football league pyramid</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_78-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Although he is predominantly known for his tactical awareness, intelligence, and the defensive aspect of his game — namely his ability to tackle and regain possession, intercept passes, and block shots — he is also capable of playmaking from inside his own half and is an efficient passer on the counter-attack. He is also quick up and down the pitch and often makes late attacking runs.<sup id="cite_ref-best_midfielder_70-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_midfielder-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-next_star_77-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-next_star-77">&#91;77&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-effective_player_79-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-effective_player-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Conte_has_made_him_better_80-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Conte_has_made_him_better-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-United_prepare_to_host_Chelsea_81-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-United_prepare_to_host_Chelsea-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kante_in_the_spotlight_82-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kante_in_the_spotlight-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-drive_83-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-drive-83">&#91;83&#93;</a></sup> He made the most tackles in Europe's top leagues, in back-to-back seasons (14–15 and 15–16,)<sup id="cite_ref-84" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-84">&#91;84&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-85" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-85">&#91;85&#93;</a></sup> and in April 2016, <a href="/wiki/Sir_Alex_Ferguson" class="mw-redirect" title="Sir Alex Ferguson">Sir Alex Ferguson</a> described him as the best player in the <a href="/wiki/Premier_League" title="Premier League">Premier League</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-best_midfielder_70-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_midfielder-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>After his first senior goal, French regional newspaper <i><a href="/wiki/La_Voix_du_Nord_(daily)" title="La Voix du Nord (daily)">La Voix du Nord</a></i> likened Kanté to <a href="/wiki/Claude_Mak%C3%A9l%C3%A9l%C3%A9" title="Claude Makélélé">Claude Makélélé</a> (in reference to his early days at <a href="/wiki/FC_Nantes" title="FC Nantes">Nantes</a>), due to their similar playing style and <a href="/wiki/Midfielder#Defensive_midfielder" title="Midfielder">defensive role in midfield</a>. After asking the player if he considered Makélélé his role model, Kanté instead said that he admired <a href="/wiki/Lassana_Diarra" title="Lassana Diarra">Lassana Diarra</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-voix_8-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-voix-8">&#91;8&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Disappointing_lack_of_deep-lying_playmakers_in_the_Premier_League_73-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Disappointing_lack_of_deep-lying_playmakers_in_the_Premier_League-73">&#91;73&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-effective_player_79-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-effective_player-79">&#91;79&#93;</a></sup> His World Cup winning midfield partner, <a href="/wiki/Paul_Pogba" title="Paul Pogba">Paul Pogba</a>, said he could outrun an entire team of 11 players.<sup id="cite_ref-United_prepare_to_host_Chelsea_81-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-United_prepare_to_host_Chelsea-81">&#91;81&#93;</a></sup> His league-title winning manager, <a href="/wiki/Claudio_Ranieri" title="Claudio Ranieri">Claudio Ranieri</a>, often joked about him having "batteries" and said: "One day, I’m going to see you cross the ball and then finish the cross with a header yourself."<sup id="cite_ref-best_midfielder_70-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-best_midfielder-70">&#91;70&#93;</a></sup> Off the pitch, Kanté's former Chelsea manager, <a href="/wiki/Antonio_Conte" title="Antonio Conte">Antonio Conte</a> praised his work ethic and constant willingness to improve.<sup id="cite_ref-Conte_has_made_him_better_80-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Conte_has_made_him_better-80">&#91;80&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Kante_in_the_spotlight_82-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Kante_in_the_spotlight-82">&#91;82&#93;</a></sup> Kanté has said he doesn't necessarily enjoy his role but the "satisfaction in recovering a ball, in protecting my team from an opponent’s attack," is what keeps him going.<sup id="cite_ref-:0_78-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup> In his first 150 Premier League appearances he totaled 92 wins, 28 losses and 10 goals. In five years, in the Premier League, he has yet to receive a red card.<sup id="cite_ref-86" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-86">&#91;86&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Personal_life">Personal life</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Personal life">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<p>Kanté was born in <a href="/wiki/Paris" title="Paris">Paris</a> to <a href="/wiki/Mali" title="Mali">Malian</a> parents who migrated to France from Mali in 1980.<sup id="cite_ref-:3_5-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:3-5">&#91;5&#93;</a></sup> He grew up in a small flat in <a href="/wiki/Rueil-Malmaison" title="Rueil-Malmaison">Rueil-Malmaison</a>, <a href="/wiki/Hauts-de-Seine" title="Hauts-de-Seine">Hauts-de-Seine</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-how_6-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-how-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> His father died shortly after N'Golo turned 11 and his elder sibling Niama died of a heart-attack before the 2018 World Cup.<sup id="cite_ref-87" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-87">&#91;87&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>He is named after King <a href="/wiki/Ngolo_Diarra" title="Ngolo Diarra">Ngolo Diarra</a> of the <a href="/wiki/Bamana_Empire" title="Bamana Empire">Bamana Empire</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-88" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-88">&#91;88&#93;</a></sup> Kanté began his career at the age of eight at JS Suresnes in the western suburbs of the capital, remaining there for a decade. His younger sister too was in the youth system at Suresnes.<sup id="cite_ref-how_6-3" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-how-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup> He was rejected from the academy at <a href="/wiki/INF_Clairefontaine" title="INF Clairefontaine">Clairefontaine</a> when he was during this time.<sup id="cite_ref-:2_17-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:2-17">&#91;17&#93;</a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Ronaldo_(Brazilian_footballer)" title="Ronaldo (Brazilian footballer)">Ronaldo</a>, <a href="/wiki/Ronaldinho" title="Ronaldinho">Ronaldinho</a> and <a href="/wiki/Diego_Maradona" title="Diego Maradona">Diego Maradona</a> were his favorite players growing up. At the age of 21, while playing for Boulogne, he earned a diploma in vocational accounting.<sup id="cite_ref-:1_89-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>At the start of his professional career at Boulogne, he commuted to training on a <a href="/wiki/Kick_scooter" title="Kick scooter">kick scooter</a> and as of 2018 drove a <a href="/wiki/Mini_Hatch" title="Mini Hatch">Mini Hatch</a> — his first purchase in England because he found it easy to learn how to drive in.<sup id="cite_ref-how_6-4" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-how-6">&#91;6&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:1_89-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:1-89">&#91;89&#93;</a></sup> He is a practising Muslim.<sup id="cite_ref-90" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-90">&#91;90&#93;</a></sup> Kanté is aware of his public perception as a shy and private individual, but also said that stories about him by current and former teammates, like <a href="/wiki/Jamie_Vardy" title="Jamie Vardy">Jamie Vardy</a>, were often exaggerated.<sup id="cite_ref-91" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-91">&#91;91&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-92" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-92">&#91;92&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-:0_78-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-:0-78">&#91;78&#93;</a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-93" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-93">&#91;93&#93;</a></sup>
</p><p>Kante's nickname is "NG" and outside of football he is an avid tennis fan, and player. He said his initiation song at Chelsea was a "stressful moment" and now his go-to karaoke song is <a href="/wiki/Vegedream" title="Vegedream">Vegedream's</a> "Ramenez La Coupe À La Maison," in which he has a verse dedicated to him.<sup id="cite_ref-94" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-94">&#91;94&#93;</a></sup> During his initiation at Chelsea, his team-mates said he was not loud enough. His favorite dish is <a href="/wiki/Thieboudienne" title="Thieboudienne">Thieboudienne</a> because of his mother's cooking.<sup id="cite_ref-95" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-95">&#91;95&#93;</a></sup>
</p>
<h2><span class="mw-headline" id="Career_statistics">Career statistics</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Career statistics">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Club">Club</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=N%27Golo_Kant%C3%A9&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Club">edit</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
